highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def position_primary_branches(root, children, radius=400):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Position first-level children in a circle around root\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    n = len(children)\n    angle_step = 2 * pi / n\n    \n    positions = []\n    for i, child in enumerate(children):\n        angle = i * angle_step\n        \n        # Calculate position on circle\n        x = root.center_x + radius * cos(angle) - child.width / 2\n        y = root.center_y + radius * sin(angle) - child.height / 2\n        \n        positions.append({\u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: x, \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: y})\n    \n    return dir=\"auto\"\u003eStep 4: Balance and Adjust\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-step-4-balance-and-adjust\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Step 4: Balance and Adjust\" href=\"#step-4-balance-and-adjust\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAfter initial placement, check for collisions and adjust:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def balance_layout(nodes):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Adjust nodes to prevent overlaps\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    max_iterations = 10\n    \n    for iteration in range(max_iterations):\n        collisions = find_all_collisions(nodes)\n        if not collisions:\n            break\n        \n        for node1, node2 in collisions:\n            # Move node2 away from node1\n            dx = node2.center_x - node1.center_x\n            dy = node2.center_y - node1.center_y\n            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)\n            \n            # Calculate required distance\n            min_dist = calculate_min_distance(node1, node2)\n            \n            if distance \u0026gt; 0:\n                # Move proportionally\n                move_x = (dx / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2\n                move_y = (dy / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2\n                \n                node2.x += move_x\n                node2.y += move_y\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ebalance_layout\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Adjust nodes to prevent overlaps\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emax_iterations\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e10\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eiteration\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003erange\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emax_iterations\u003c/span\u003e):\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecollisions\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003efind_all_collisions\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e)\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003enot\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecollisions\u003c/span\u003e:\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ebreak\u003c/span\u003e\n        \n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode1\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode2\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecollisions\u003c/span\u003e:\n            \u003cspan data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def position_tree_layout(root, tree):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Top-down tree layout\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # Level 0 (root)\n    root.x = 0 - root.width / 2\n    root.y = 0 - root.height / 2\n    \n    # Process each level\n    for level in range(1, max_depth):\n        nodes_at_level = get_nodes_at_level(tree, level)\n        \n        # Calculate horizontal spacing\n        total_width = sum(node.width for node in nodes_at_level)\n        total_spacing = (len(nodes_at_level) - 1) * HORIZONTAL_SPACING\n        \n        start_x = -(total_width + total_spacing) / 2\n        y = level * (150 + VERTICAL_SPACING)  # 150px level height\n        \n        current_x = start_x\n        for node in nodes_at_level:\n            node.x = current_x\n            node.y = y\n            current_x += node.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def layout_zones(groups, canvas_width=2000, canvas_height=1500):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Arrange groups in grid zones\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    n_groups = len(groups)\n    \n    # Calculate grid dimensions\n    cols = ceil(sqrt(n_groups))\n    rows = ceil(n_groups / cols)\n    \n    zone_width = canvas_width / cols\n    zone_height = canvas_height / rows\n    \n    # Assign zones\n    zones = []\n    for i, group in enumerate(groups):\n        col = i % cols\n        row = i // cols\n        \n        zone = {\n            \u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: col * zone_width - canvas_width / 2,\n            \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: row * zone_height - canvas_height / 2,\n            \u0026quot;width\u0026quot;: zone_width * 0.9,  # Leave 10% margin\n            \u0026quot;height\u0026quot;: zone_height * 0.9,\n            \u0026quot;group\u0026quot;: group\n        }\n        zones.append(zone)\n    \n    return zones\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def position_organic(zone, nodes):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Organic, flowing arrangement within zone\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    positions = []\n    \n    # Start at zone top-left with margin\n    current_x = zone.x + 50\n    current_y = zone.y + 50\n    row_height = 0\n    \n    for node in nodes:\n        # Check if node VERTICAL_SPACING\n            row_height = 0\n        \n        positions.append({\n            \u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: current_x,\n            \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: current_y\n        })\n class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def position_grid(zone, nodes):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Grid arrangement within zone\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    n = len(nodes)\n    cols = ceil(sqrt(n))\n    rows = ceil(n / cols)\n    \n    cell_width = (zone.width - 100) / cols  # 50px margin each side\n    cell_height = (zone.height - 100) / rows\n    \n    positions = []\n    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):\n        col = i % cols\n        row = i // cols\n        \n        # Center node in cell\n        x = zone.x + 50 + col * cell_width + (cell_width - node.width) / 2\n        y = zone.y + 50 + row * cell_height + (cell_height - node.height) / 2\n        \n        positions.append({\u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: x, \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: y})\n    \n    return positions\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def calculate_edge_path(from_node, to_node):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Determine edge connection points\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # Calculate centers\n    from_center = (from_node.x + from_node.width/2, \n                   from_node.y + from_node.height/2)\n    to_center = (to_node.x + to_node.width/2,\n                 to_node.y + to_node.height/2)\n    \n    # Determine best sides to connect\n    dx = to_center[0] - from_center[0]\n    dy = to_center[1] - from_center[1]\n    \n    # Choose sides based on direction\n    if abs(dx) \u0026gt; abs(dy):\n        # Horizontal connection\n        from_side = \u0026quot;right\u0026quot; if dx \u0026gt; 0 else \u0026quot;left\u0026quot;\n        to_side = \u0026quot;left\u0026quot; if dx \u0026gt; 0 else \u0026quot;right\u0026quot;\n    else:\n        # Vertical connection\n        from_side = \u0026quot;bottom\u0026quot; if dy \u0026gt; 0 else \u0026quot;top\u0026quot;\n        to_side = \u0026quot;top\u0026quot; if dy \u0026gt; 0 else \u0026quot;bottom\u0026quot;\n    \n    return {\n        \u0026quot;fromSide\u0026quot;: from_side,\n        \u0026quot;toSide\u0026quot;: to_side\n    }\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 dir=\"auto\"\u003eForce-Directed Layout\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-force-directed-layout\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Force-Directed Layout\" href=\"#force-directed-layout\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor complex networks with many cross-connections:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def force_directed_layout(nodes, edges, iterations=100):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Spring-based layout algorithm\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # Constants\n    SPRING_LENGTH = 200\n    SPRING_CONSTANT = 0.1\n    REPULSION_CONSTANT = 5000\n    \n    for iteration in range(iterations):\n        # Calculate repulsive forces (all pairs)\n        for node1 in nodes:\n            force_x, force_y = 0, 0\n            \n            for node2 in nodes:\n                if node1 == node2:\n                    continue\n                \n                dx = node1.x - node2.x\n                dy = node1.y - node2.y\n                distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)\n                \n                if distance \u0026gt; 0:\n                    # Repulsive force\n                    force = REPULSION_CONSTANT / (distance * distance)\n                    force_x += (dx / distance) * force\n                    force_y += (dy / distance) * force\n            \n            node1.force_x = force_x\n            node1.force_y = force_y\n        \n        # Calculate attractive forces (connected nodes)\n        for edge in edges:\n            node1 = get_node(edge.fromNode)\n            node2 = get_node(edge.toNode)\n            \n            dx = node2.x - node1.x\n            dy = node2.y - node1.y\n            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)\n            \n            # Spring force\n            force = SPRING_CONSTANT * (distance - SPRING_LENGTH)\n            \n            node1.force_x += (dx / distance) * force\n            node1.force_y += (dy / distance) * force\n            node2.force_x -= (dx / distance) * force\n            node2.force_y -= (dy / distance) * force\n        \n        # Apply forces\n        for node in nodes:\n            node.x += node.force_x\n            node.y += node.force_y\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eforce_directed_layout\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eedges\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eiterations\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e100\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Spring-based layout algorithm\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Constants\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eSPRING_LENGTH\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e200\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eSPRING_CONSTANT\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0.1\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eREPULSION_CONSTANT\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e5000\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eiteration\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003erange\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eiterations\u003c/span\u003e):\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Calculate repulsive forces (all pairs)\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode1\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e:\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eforce_x\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eforce_y\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e\n            \n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode2\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e:\n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode1\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e==\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode2\u003c/span\u003e:\n                    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003econtinue\u003c/span\u003e\n                \n                \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003edx\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode1\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eGroup related nodes automatically:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def hierarchical_cluster(nodes, similarity_threshold=0.7):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Cluster nodes by content similarity\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    clusters = []\n    \n    # Calculate similarity matrix\n    similarity = calculate_similarity_matrix(nodes)\n    \n    # Agglomerative clustering\n    current_clusters = [[node] for node in nodes]\n    \n    while len(current_clusters) \u0026gt; 1:\n        # Find most similar clusters\n        max_sim = 0\n        merge_i, merge_j = 0, 1\n        \n        for i in range(len(current_clusters)):\n            for j in range(i + 1, len(current_clusters)):\n                sim = cluster_similarity(current_clusters[i], \n                                       current_clusters[j], \n                                       similarity)\n                if sim \u0026gt; max_sim:\n                    max_sim = sim\n                    merge_i, merge_j = i, j\n        \n        if max_sim \u0026lt; similarity_threshold:\n            break\n        \n        # Merge clusters\n        current_clusters[merge_i].extend(current_clusters[merge_j])\n        current_clusters.pop(merge_j)\n    \n    return current_clusters\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ehierarchical_cluster\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003esimilarity_threshold\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0.7\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Cluster nodes by content similarity\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eclusters\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e []\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Calculate similarity matrix\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003esimilarity\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ecalculate_similarity_matrix\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e)\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Agglomerative clustering\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecurrent_clusters\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e [[\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode\u003c/span\u003e] \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efor\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enode\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ein\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003enodes\u003c/span\u003e]\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ewhile\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003elen\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecurrent_clusters\u003c/span\u003e) \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e1\u003c/span\u003e:\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Find most similar clusters\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emax_sim\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emerge_i\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003emerge_j\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e0\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def minimize_crossings(nodes, edges):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Reduce edge crossing through node repositioning\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    crossings = count_crossings(edges)\n    \n    # Try swapping adjacent nodes\n    improved = True\n    while improved:\n        improved = False\n        \n        for i in range(len(nodes) - 1):\n            # Swap nodes i and i+1\n            swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])\n            new_crossings = count_crossings(edges)\n            \n            if new_crossings \u0026lt; crossings:\n                crossings = new_crossings\n                improved = True\n            else:\n                # Swap back\n                swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eminimize_crossings\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def calculate_visual_weight(canvas):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Calculate center of mass for visual balance\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    total_weight = 0\n    weighted_x = 0\n    weighted_y = 0\n    \n    for node in canvas.nodes:\n        # Weight is proportional to area\n        weight = node.width * node.height\n        total_weight += weight\n        \n        weighted_x += node.center_x * weight\n        weighted_y += node.center_y * weight\n    \n    center_x = weighted_x / total_weight\n    center_y = weighted_y / total_weight\n    \n    # Shift entire canvas to center at (0, 0)\n    offset_x = -center_x\n    offset_y = -center_y\n    \n    for node in canvas.nodes:\n        node.x += offset_x\n        node.y += offset_y\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan href=\"#spatial-indexing\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor large canvases, use spatial indexing to speed up collision detection:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"class SpatialGrid:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Grid-based spatial index for fast collision detection\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    \n    def __init__(self, cell_size=500):\n        self.cell_size = cell_size\n        self.grid = {}\n    \n    def add_node(self, node):\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Add node to grid\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        cells = self.get_cells(node)\n        for cell in cells:\n            if cell not in self.grid:\n                self.grid[cell] = []\n            self.grid[cell].append(node)\n    \n    def get_cells(self, node):\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get grid cells node occupies\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        min_x = int(node.x / self.cell_size)\n        max_x = int((node.x + node.width) / self.cell_size)\n        min_y = int(node.y / self.cell_size)\n        max_y = int((node.y + node.height) / self.cell_size)\n        \n        cells = []\n        for x in range(min_x, max_x + 1):\n            for y in range(min_y, max_y + 1):\n                cells.append((x, y))\n        return cells\n    \n    def get_nearby_nodes(self, node):\n        \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Get nodes in nearby cells\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n        cells = self.get_cells(node)\n        nearby = set()\n        \n        for cell in cells:\n            if cell in self.grid:\n                nearby.update(self.grid[cell])\n        \n        return nearby\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eclass\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eSpatialGrid\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Grid-based spatial index for fast collision detection\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003e__init__\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def layout_timeline(events, direction=\u0026quot;horizontal\u0026quot;):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Create timeline layout\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    if direction == \u0026quot;horizontal\u0026quot;:\n        for i, event in enumerate(events):\n Layout Algorithms for Obsidian Canvas","","Detailed algorithms for positioning nodes in MindMap and Freeform layouts.","","## Layout Principles","","### Universal Spacing Constants","","```","HORIZONTAL_SPACING = 320  // Minimum horizontal space between node centers","VERTICAL_SPACING = 200    // Minimum vertical space between node centers","NODE_PADDING = 20         // Internal padding within nodes","```","","### Collision Detection","","Before finalizing any node position, verify:","","```python","def check_collision(node1, node2):","    \"\"\"Returns True if nodes overlap or are too close\"\"\"","    center1_x = node1.x + node1.width / 2","    center1_y = node1.y + node1.height / 2","    center2_x = node2.x + node2.width / 2","    center2_y = node2.y + node2.height / 2","    ","    dx = abs(center1_x - center2_x)","    dy = abs(center1_y - center2_y)","    ","    min_dx = (node1.width + node2.width) / 2 + HORIZONTAL_SPACING","    min_dy = (node1.height + node2.height) / 2 + VERTICAL_SPACING","    ","    return dx \u003c min_dx or dy \u003c min_dy","```","","## MindMap Layout Algorithm","","### 1. Radial Tree Layout","","Place root at center, arrange children radially.","","#### Step 1: Position Root Node","","```python","root = {","    \"x\": 0 - (root_width / 2),  # Center horizontally","    \"y\": 0 - (root_height / 2), # Center vertically","    \"width\": root_width,","    \"height\": root_height","}","```","","#### Step 2: Calculate Primary Branch Positions","","Distribute first-level children around root:","","```python","def position_primary_branches(root, children, radius=400):","    \"\"\"Position first-level children in a circle around root\"\"\"","    n = len(children)","    angle_step = 2 * pi / n","    ","    positions = []","    for i, child in enumerate(children):","        angle = i * angle_step","        ","        # Calculate position on circle","        x = root.center_x + radius * cos(angle) - child.width / 2","        y = root.center_y + radius * sin(angle) - child.height / 2","        ","        positions.append({\"x\": x, \"y\": y})","    ","    return positions","```","","**Radius Selection:**","- Small canvases (≤10 children): 400px","- Medium canvases (11-20 children): 500px","- Large canvases (\u003e20 children): 600px","","#### Step 3: Position Secondary Branches","","For each primary branch, arrange its children:","","**Horizontal Layout** (preferred for most cases):","","```python","def position_secondary_horizontal(parent, children, distance=350):","    \"\"\"Arrange children horizontally to the right of parent\"\"\"","    n = len(children)","    total_height = sum(child.height for child in children)","    total_spacing = (n - 1) * VERTICAL_SPACING","    ","    # Start position (top of vertical arrangement)","    start_y = parent.center_y - (total_height + total_spacing) / 2","    ","    positions = []","    current_y = start_y","    ","    for child in children:","        x = parent.x + parent.width + distance","        y = current_y","        ","        positions.append({\"x\": x, \"y\": y})","        current_y += child.height + VERTICAL_SPACING","    ","    return positions","```","","**Vertical Layout** (for left/right primary branches):","","```python","def position_secondary_vertical(parent, children, distance=250):","    \"\"\"Arrange children vertically below parent\"\"\"","    n = len(children)","    total_width = sum(child.width for child in children)","    total_spacing = (n - 1) * HORIZONTAL_SPACING","    ","    # Start position (left of horizontal arrangement)","    start_x = parent.center_x - (total_width + total_spacing) / 2","    ","    positions = []","    current_x = start_x","    ","    for child in children:","        x = current_x","        y = parent.y + parent.height + distance","        ","        positions.append({\"x\": x, \"y\": y})","        current_x += child.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING","    ","    return positions","```","","#### Step 4: Balance and Adjust","","After initial placement, check for collisions and adjust:","","```python","def balance_layout(nodes):","    \"\"\"Adjust nodes to prevent overlaps\"\"\"","    max_iterations = 10","    ","    for iteration in range(max_iterations):","        collisions = find_all_collisions(nodes)","        if not collisions:","            break","        ","        for node1, node2 in collisions:","            # Move node2 away from node1","            dx = node2.center_x - node1.center_x","            dy = node2.center_y - node1.center_y","            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)","            ","            # Calculate required distance","            min_dist = calculate_min_distance(node1, node2)","            ","            if distance \u003e 0:","                # Move proportionally","                move_x = (dx / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2","                move_y = (dy / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2","                ","                node2.x += move_x","                node2.y += move_y","```","","### 2. Tree Layout (Hierarchical Top-Down)","","Alternative for deep hierarchies.","","#### Positioning Formula","","```python","def position_tree_layout(root, tree):","    \"\"\"Top-down tree layout\"\"\"","    # Level 0 (root)","    root.x = 0 - root.width / 2","    root.y = 0 - root.height / 2","    ","    # Process each level","    for level in range(1, max_depth):","        nodes_at_level = get_nodes_at_level(tree, level)","        ","        # Calculate horizontal spacing","        total_width = sum(node.width for node in nodes_at_level)","        total_spacing = (len(nodes_at_level) - 1) * HORIZONTAL_SPACING","        ","        start_x = -(total_width + total_spacing) / 2","        y = level * (150 + VERTICAL_SPACING)  # 150px level height","        ","        current_x = start_x","        for node in nodes_at_level:","            node.x = current_x","            node.y = y","            current_x += node.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING","```","","## Freeform Layout Algorithm","","### 1. Content-Based Grouping","","First, identify natural groupings in content:","","```python","def identify_groups(nodes, content_structure):","    \"\"\"Group nodes by semantic relationships\"\"\"","    groups = []","    ","    # Analyze content structure","    for section in content_structure:","        group_nodes = [node for node in nodes if node.section == section]","        ","        if len(group_nodes) \u003e 1:","            groups.append({","                \"label\": section.title,","                \"nodes\": group_nodes","            })","    ","    return groups","```","","### 2. Grid-Based Zone Layout","","Divide canvas into zones for different groups:","","```python","def layout_zones(groups, canvas_width=2000, canvas_height=1500):","    \"\"\"Arrange groups in grid zones\"\"\"","    n_groups = len(groups)","    ","    # Calculate grid dimensions","    cols = ceil(sqrt(n_groups))","    rows = ceil(n_groups / cols)","    ","    zone_width = canvas_width / cols","    zone_height = canvas_height / rows","    ","    # Assign zones","    zones = []","    for i, group in enumerate(groups):","        col = i % cols","        row = i // cols","        ","        zone = {","            \"x\": col * zone_width - canvas_width / 2,","            \"y\": row * zone_height - canvas_height / 2,","            \"width\": zone_width * 0.9,  # Leave 10% margin","            \"height\": zone_height * 0.9,","            \"group\": group","        }","        zones.append(zone)","    ","    return zones","```","","### 3. Within-Zone Node Positioning","","Position nodes within each zone:","","**Option A: Organic Flow**","","```python","def position_organic(zone, nodes):","    \"\"\"Organic, flowing arrangement within zone\"\"\"","    positions = []","    ","    # Start at zone top-left with margin","    current_x = zone.x + 50","    current_y = zone.y + 50","    row_height = 0","    ","    for node in nodes:","        # Check if node fits in current row","        if current_x + node.width \u003e zone.x + zone.width - 50:","            # Move to next row","            current_x = zone.x + 50","            current_y += row_height + VERTICAL_SPACING","            row_height = 0","        ","        positions.append({","            \"x\": current_x,","            \"y\": current_y","        })","        ","        current_x += node.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING","        row_height = max(row_height, node.height)","    ","    return positions","```","","**Option B: Structured Grid**","","```python","def position_grid(zone, nodes):","    \"\"\"Grid arrangement within zone\"\"\"","    n = len(nodes)","    cols = ceil(sqrt(n))","    rows = ceil(n / cols)","    ","    cell_width = (zone.width - 100) / cols  # 50px margin each side","    cell_height = (zone.height - 100) / rows","    ","    positions = []","    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):","        col = i % cols","        row = i // cols","        ","        # Center node in cell","        x = zone.x + 50 + col * cell_width + (cell_width - node.width) / 2","        y = zone.y + 50 + row * cell_height + (cell_height - node.height) / 2","        ","        positions.append({\"x\": x, \"y\": y})","    ","    return positions","```","","### 4. Cross-Zone Connections","","Calculate optimal edge paths between zones:","","```python","def calculate_edge_path(from_node, to_node):","    \"\"\"Determine edge connection points\"\"\"","    # Calculate centers","    from_center = (from_node.x + from_node.width/2, ","                   from_node.y + from_node.height/2)","    to_center = (to_node.x + to_node.width/2,","                 to_node.y + to_node.height/2)","    ","    # Determine best sides to connect","    dx = to_center[0] - from_center[0]","    dy = to_center[1] - from_center[1]","    ","    # Choose sides based on direction","    if abs(dx) \u003e abs(dy):","        # Horizontal connection","        from_side = \"right\" if dx \u003e 0 else \"left\"","        to_side = \"left\" if dx \u003e 0 else \"right\"","    else:","        # Vertical connection","        from_side = \"bottom\" if dy \u003e 0 else \"top\"","        to_side = \"top\" if dy \u003e 0 else \"bottom\"","    ","    return {","        \"fromSide\": from_side,","        \"toSide\": to_side","    }","```","","## Advanced Techniques","","### Force-Directed Layout","","For complex networks with many cross-connections:","","```python","def force_directed_layout(nodes, edges, iterations=100):","    \"\"\"Spring-based layout algorithm\"\"\"","    # Constants","    SPRING_LENGTH = 200","    SPRING_CONSTANT = 0.1","    REPULSION_CONSTANT = 5000","    ","    for iteration in range(iterations):","        # Calculate repulsive forces (all pairs)","        for node1 in nodes:","            force_x, force_y = 0, 0","            ","            for node2 in nodes:","                if node1 == node2:","                    continue","                ","                dx = node1.x - node2.x","                dy = node1.y - node2.y","                distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)","                ","                if distance \u003e 0:","                    # Repulsive force","                    force = REPULSION_CONSTANT / (distance * distance)","                    force_x += (dx / distance) * force","                    force_y += (dy / distance) * force","            ","            node1.force_x = force_x","            node1.force_y = force_y","        ","        # Calculate attractive forces (connected nodes)","        for edge in edges:","            node1 = get_node(edge.fromNode)","            node2 = get_node(edge.toNode)","            ","            dx = node2.x - node1.x","            dy = node2.y - node1.y","            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)","            ","            # Spring force","            force = SPRING_CONSTANT * (distance - SPRING_LENGTH)","            ","            node1.force_x += (dx / distance) * force","            node1.force_y += (dy / distance) * force","            node2.force_x -= (dx / distance) * force","            node2.force_y -= (dy / distance) * force","        ","        # Apply forces","        for node in nodes:","            node.x += node.force_x","            node.y += node.force_y","```","","### Hierarchical Clustering","","Group related nodes automatically:","","```python","def hierarchical_cluster(nodes, similarity_threshold=0.7):","    \"\"\"Cluster nodes by content similarity\"\"\"","    clusters = []","    ","    # Calculate similarity matrix","    similarity = calculate_similarity_matrix(nodes)","    ","    # Agglomerative clustering","    current_clusters = [[node] for node in nodes]","    ","    while len(current_clusters) \u003e 1:","        # Find most similar clusters","        max_sim = 0","        merge_i, merge_j = 0, 1","        ","        for i in range(len(current_clusters)):","            for j in range(i + 1, len(current_clusters)):","                sim = cluster_similarity(current_clusters[i], ","                                       current_clusters[j], ","                                       similarity)","                if sim \u003e max_sim:","                    max_sim = sim","                    merge_i, merge_j = i, j","        ","        if max_sim \u003c similarity_threshold:","            break","        ","        # Merge clusters","        current_clusters[merge_i].extend(current_clusters[merge_j])","        current_clusters.pop(merge_j)","    ","    return current_clusters","```","","## Layout Optimization","","### Minimize Edge Crossings","","```python","def minimize_crossings(nodes, edges):","    \"\"\"Reduce edge crossing through node repositioning\"\"\"","    crossings = count_crossings(edges)","    ","    # Try swapping adjacent nodes","    improved = True","    while improved:","        improved = False","        ","        for i in range(len(nodes) - 1):","            # Swap nodes i and i+1","            swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])","            new_crossings = count_crossings(edges)","            ","            if new_crossings \u003c crossings:","                crossings = new_crossings","                improved = True","            else:","                # Swap back","                swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])","```","","### Visual Balance","","```python","def calculate_visual_weight(canvas):","    \"\"\"Calculate center of mass for visual balance\"\"\"","    total_weight = 0","    weighted_x = 0","    weighted_y = 0","    ","    for node in canvas.nodes:","        # Weight is proportional to area","        weight = node.width * node.height","        total_weight += weight","        ","        weighted_x += node.center_x * weight","        weighted_y += node.center_y * weight","    ","    center_x = weighted_x / total_weight","    center_y = weighted_y / total_weight","    ","    # Shift entire canvas to center at (0, 0)","    offset_x = -center_x","    offset_y = -center_y","    ","    for node in canvas.nodes:","        node.x += offset_x","        node.y += offset_y","```","","## Performance Optimization","","### Spatial Indexing","","For large canvases, use spatial indexing to speed up collision detection:","","```python","class SpatialGrid:","    \"\"\"Grid-based spatial index for fast collision detection\"\"\"","    ","    def __init__(self, cell_size=500):","        self.cell_size = cell_size","        self.grid = {}","    ","    def add_node(self, node):","        \"\"\"Add node to grid\"\"\"","        cells = self.get_cells(node)","        for cell in cells:","            if cell not in self.grid:","                self.grid[cell] = []","            self.grid[cell].append(node)","    ","    def get_cells(self, node):","        \"\"\"Get grid cells node occupies\"\"\"","        min_x = int(node.x / self.cell_size)","        max_x = int((node.x + node.width) / self.cell_size)","        min_y = int(node.y / self.cell_size)","        max_y = int((node.y + node.height) / self.cell_size)","        ","        cells = []","        for x in range(min_x, max_x + 1):","            for y in range(min_y, max_y + 1):","                cells.append((x, y))","        return cells","    ","    def get_nearby_nodes(self, node):","        \"\"\"Get nodes in nearby cells\"\"\"","        cells = self.get_cells(node)","        nearby = set()","        ","        for cell in cells:","            if cell in self.grid:","                nearby.update(self.grid[cell])","        ","        return nearby","```","","## Common Layout Patterns","","### Timeline Layout","","For chronological content:","","```python","def layout_timeline(events, direction=\"horizontal\"):","    \"\"\"Create timeline layout\"\"\"","    if direction == \"horizontal\":","        for i, event in enumerate(events):","            event.x = i * (event.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING)","            event.y = 0","    else:  # vertical","        for i, event in enumerate(events):","            event.x = 0","            event.y = i * (event.height + VERTICAL_SPACING)","```","","### Circular Layout","","For cyclical processes:","","```python","def layout_circular(nodes, radius=500):","    \"\"\"Arrange nodes in a circle\"\"\"","    n = len(nodes)","    angle_step = 2 * pi / n","    ","    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):","        angle = i * angle_step","        node.x = radius * cos(angle) - node.width / 2","        node.y = radius * sin(angle) - node.height / 2","```","","### Matrix Layout","","For comparing multiple dimensions:","","```python","def layout_matrix(nodes, rows, cols):","    \"\"\"Arrange nodes in a matrix\"\"\"","    cell_width = 400","    cell_height = 250","    ","    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):","        row = i // cols","        col = i % cols","        ","        node.x = col * cell_width","        node.y = row * cell_height","```","","## Quality Checks","","Before finalizing layout, verify:","","1. **No Overlaps**: All nodes have minimum spacing","2. **Balanced**: Visual center near (0, 0)","3. **Accessible**: All nodes reachable via edges","4. **Readable**: Text sizes appropriate for zoom level","5. **Efficient**: Edge paths reasonably direct","","Use these <p dir="auto">Detailed algorithms for positioning nodes in MindMap and Freeform layouts.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Layout Principles</h2><a id="user-content-layout-principles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Layout Principles" href="#layout-principles"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Universal Spacing Constants</h3><a id="user-content-universal-spacing-constants" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Universal Spacing Constants" href="#universal-spacing-constants"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="HORIZONTAL_SPACING = 320  // Minimum horizontal space between node centers

NODE_PADDING = 20         // Internal padding within nodes"><pre class="notranslate"><code>HORIZONTAL_SPACING = 320  // Minimum horizontal space between node centers
VERTICAL_SPACING = 200    // Minimum vertical space between node centers
NODE_PADDING = 20         // Internal padding within nodes
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Collision Detection</h3><a id="user-content-collision-detection" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Collision Detection" href="#collision-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before finalizing any node position, verify:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def check_collision(node1, node2):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Returns True if nodes overlap or are too close&quot;&quot;&quot;
    center1_x = node1.x + node1.width / 2
    center1_y = node1.y + node1.height / 2
    center2_x = node2.x + node2.width / 2
    center2_y = node2.y + node2.height / 2
    
    dx = abs(center1_x - center2_x)
    dy = abs(center1_y - center2_y)
    
    min_dx = (node1.width + node2.width) / 2 + HORIZONTAL_SPACING
    min_dy = (node1.height + node2.height) / 2 + VERTICAL_SPACING
    
    return dx &lt; min_dx or dy &lt; min_dy"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">check_collision</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Returns True if nodes overlap or are too close"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">center1_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">center1_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">center2_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">center2_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">abs</span>(<span class="pl-s1">center1_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">center2_x</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">abs</span>(<span class="pl-s1">center1_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">center2_y</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-s1">min_dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">min_dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">min_dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">or</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">min_dy</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">MindMap Layout Algorithm</h2><a id="user-content-mindmap-layout-algorithm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: MindMap Layout Algorithm" href="#mindmap-layout-algorithm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Radial Tree Layout</h3><a id="user-content-1-radial-tree-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Radial Tree Layout" href="#1-radial-tree-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Place root at center, arrange children radially.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Position Root Node</h4><a id="user-content-step-1-position-root-node" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Position Root Node" href="#step-1-position-root-node"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="root = {
    &quot;x&quot;: 0 - (root_width / 2),  # Center horizontally
    &quot;y&quot;: 0 - (root_height / 2), # Center vertically
    &quot;width&quot;: root_width,
    &quot;height&quot;: root_height
}"><pre><span class="pl-s1">root</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {
    <span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> (<span class="pl-s1">root_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>),  <span class="pl-c"># Center horizontally</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> (<span class="pl-s1">root_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>), <span class="pl-c"># Center vertically</span>
    <span class="pl-s">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">root_width</span>,
    <span class="pl-s">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">root_height</span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Calculate Primary Branch Positions</h4><a id="user-content-step-2-calculate-primary-branch-positions" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Calculate Primary Branch Positions" href="#step-2-calculate-primary-branch-positions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Distribute first-level children around root:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_primary_branches(root, children, radius=400):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Position first-level children in a circle around root&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n = len(children)
    angle_step = 2 * pi / n
    
    positions = []
    for i, child in enumerate(children):
        angle = i * angle_step
        
        # Calculate position on circle
        x = root.center_x + radius * cos(angle) - child.width / 2
        y = root.center_y + radius * sin(angle) - child.height / 2
        
        positions.append({&quot;x&quot;: x, &quot;y&quot;: y})
    
    return positions"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_primary_branches</span>(<span class="pl-s1">root</span>, <span class="pl-s1">children</span>, <span class="pl-s1">radius</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">400</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Position first-level children in a circle around root"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">children</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">angle_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">pi</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">n</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">positions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">children</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">angle</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">angle_step</span>
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Calculate position on circle</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-en">cos</span>(<span class="pl-s1">angle</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-en">sin</span>(<span class="pl-s1">angle</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">positions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({<span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">y</span>})
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">positions</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Radius Selection:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Small canvases (≤10 children): 400px</li>
<li>Medium canvases (11-20 children): 500px</li>
<li>Large canvases (&gt;20 children): 600px</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Position Secondary Branches</h4><a id="user-content-step-3-position-secondary-branches" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Position Secondary Branches" href="#step-3-position-secondary-branches"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For each primary branch, arrange its children:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Horizontal Layout</strong> (preferred for most cases):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_secondary_horizontal(parent, children, distance=350):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Arrange children horizontally to the right of parent&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n = len(children)
    total_height = sum(child.height for child in children)
    total_spacing = (n - 1) * VERTICAL_SPACING
    
    # Start position (top of vertical arrangement)
    start_y = parent.center_y - (total_height + total_spacing) / 2
    
    positions = []
    current_y = start_y
    
    for child in children:
        x = parent.x + parent.width + distance
        y = current_y
        
        positions.append({&quot;x&quot;: x, &quot;y&quot;: y})
        current_y += child.height + VERTICAL_SPACING
    
    return positions"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_secondary_horizontal</span>(<span class="pl-s1">parent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">children</span>, <span class="pl-s1">distance</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">350</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Arrange children horizontally to the right of parent"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">children</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">total_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(<span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">children</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Start position (top of vertical arrangement)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">start_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> (<span class="pl-s1">total_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">positions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">start_y</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">children</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">positions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({<span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">y</span>})
        <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">positions</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Vertical Layout</strong> (for left/right primary branches):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_secondary_vertical(parent, children, distance=250):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Arrange children vertically below parent&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n = len(children)
    total_width = sum(child.width for child in children)
    total_spacing = (n - 1) * HORIZONTAL_SPACING
    
    # Start position (left of horizontal arrangement)
    start_x = parent.center_x - (total_width + total_spacing) / 2
    
    positions = []
    current_x = start_x
    
    for child in children:
        x = current_x
        y = parent.y + parent.height + distance
        
        positions.append({&quot;x&quot;: x, &quot;y&quot;: y})
        current_x += child.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING
    
    return positions"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_secondary_vertical</span>(<span class="pl-s1">parent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">children</span>, <span class="pl-s1">distance</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">250</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Arrange children vertically below parent"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">children</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">total_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(<span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">children</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Start position (left of horizontal arrangement)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">start_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> (<span class="pl-s1">total_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">positions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">start_x</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">children</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">parent</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">positions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({<span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">y</span>})
        <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">child</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">positions</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4: Balance and Adjust</h4><a id="user-content-step-4-balance-and-adjust" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4: Balance and Adjust" href="#step-4-balance-and-adjust"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After initial placement, check for collisions and adjust:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def balance_layout(nodes):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Adjust nodes to prevent overlaps&quot;&quot;&quot;
    max_iterations = 10
    
    for iteration in range(max_iterations):
        collisions = find_all_collisions(nodes)
        if not collisions:
            break
        
        for node1, node2 in collisions:
            # Move node2 away from node1
            dx = node2.center_x - node1.center_x
            dy = node2.center_y - node1.center_y
            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)
            
            # Calculate required distance
            min_dist = calculate_min_distance(node1, node2)
            
            if distance &gt; 0:
                # Move proportionally
                move_x = (dx / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2
                move_y = (dy / distance) * (min_dist - distance) / 2
                
                node2.x += move_x
                node2.y += move_y"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">balance_layout</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Adjust nodes to prevent overlaps"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">max_iterations</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">10</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">iteration</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">max_iterations</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">collisions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">find_all_collisions</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">collisions</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">break</span>
        
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node2</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">collisions</span>:
            <span class="pl-c"># Move node2 away from node1</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_x</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_y</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sqrt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dx</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dy</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-c"># Calculate required distance</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">min_dist</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">calculate_min_distance</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
                <span class="pl-c"># Move proportionally</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">move_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-s1">min_dist</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">move_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-s1">min_dist</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
                
                <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">move_x</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">move_y</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Tree Layout (Hierarchical Top-Down)</h3><a id="user-content-2-tree-layout-hierarchical-top-down" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Tree Layout (Hierarchical Top-Down)" href="#2-tree-layout-hierarchical-top-down"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternative for deep hierarchies.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Positioning Formula</h4><a id="user-content-positioning-formula" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Positioning Formula" href="#positioning-formula"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_tree_layout(root, tree):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Top-down tree layout&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # Level 0 (root)
    root.x = 0 - root.width / 2
    root.y = 0 - root.height / 2
    
    # Process each level
    for level in range(1, max_depth):
        nodes_at_level = get_nodes_at_level(tree, level)
        
        # Calculate horizontal spacing
        total_width = sum(node.width for node in nodes_at_level)
        total_spacing = (len(nodes_at_level) - 1) * HORIZONTAL_SPACING
        
        start_x = -(total_width + total_spacing) / 2
        y = level * (150 + VERTICAL_SPACING)  # 150px level height
        
        current_x = start_x
        for node in nodes_at_level:
            node.x = current_x
            node.y = y
            current_x += node.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_tree_layout</span>(<span class="pl-s1">root</span>, <span class="pl-s1">tree</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Top-down tree layout"""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Level 0 (root)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">root</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Process each level</span>
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">level</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">max_depth</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">nodes_at_level</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_nodes_at_level</span>(<span class="pl-s1">tree</span>, <span class="pl-s1">level</span>)
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Calculate horizontal spacing</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">total_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sum</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes_at_level</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes_at_level</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">start_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span>(<span class="pl-s1">total_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">total_spacing</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">level</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-c1">150</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># 150px level height</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">start_x</span>
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes_at_level</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Freeform Layout Algorithm</h2><a id="user-content-freeform-layout-algorithm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Freeform Layout Algorithm" href="#freeform-layout-algorithm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Content-Based Grouping</h3><a id="user-content-1-content-based-grouping" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Content-Based Grouping" href="#1-content-based-grouping"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">First, identify natural groupings in content:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def identify_groups(nodes, content_structure):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Group nodes by semantic relationships&quot;&quot;&quot;
    groups = []
    
    # Analyze content structure
    for section in content_structure:
        group_nodes = [node for node in nodes if node.section == section]
        
        if len(group_nodes) &gt; 1:
            groups.append({
                &quot;label&quot;: section.title,
                &quot;nodes&quot;: group_nodes
            })
    
    return groups"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">identify_groups</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">content_structure</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Group nodes by semantic relationships"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">groups</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Analyze content structure</span>
