    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">section</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">content_structure</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">group_nodes</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [<span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">section</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s1">section</span>]
        
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">group_nodes</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">groups</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({
                <span class="pl-s">"label"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">section</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span>,
                <span class="pl-s">"nodes"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">group_nodes</span>
            })
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">groups</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Grid-Based Zone Layout</h3><a id="user-content-2-grid-based-zone-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Grid-Based Zone Layout" href="#2-grid-based-zone-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Divide canvas into zones for different groups:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def layout_zones(groups, canvas_width=2000, canvas_height=1500):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Arrange groups in grid zones&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n_groups = len(groups)
    
    # Calculate grid dimensions
    cols = ceil(sqrt(n_groups))
    rows = ceil(n_groups / cols)
    
    zone_width = canvas_width / cols
    zone_height = canvas_height / rows
    
    # Assign zones
    zones = []
    for i, group in enumerate(groups):
        col = i % cols
        row = i // cols
        
        zone = {
            &quot;x&quot;: col * zone_width - canvas_width / 2,
            &quot;y&quot;: row * zone_height - canvas_height / 2,
            &quot;width&quot;: zone_width * 0.9,  # Leave 10% margin
            &quot;height&quot;: zone_height * 0.9,
            &quot;group&quot;: group
        }
        zones.append(zone)
    
    return zones"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">layout_zones</span>(<span class="pl-s1">groups</span>, <span class="pl-s1">canvas_width</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">2000</span>, <span class="pl-s1">canvas_height</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1500</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Arrange groups in grid zones"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n_groups</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">groups</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Calculate grid dimensions</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cols</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ceil</span>(<span class="pl-en">sqrt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_groups</span>))
    <span class="pl-s1">rows</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ceil</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n_groups</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-s1">zone_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">zone_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">rows</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Assign zones</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">zones</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">group</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">groups</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">//</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">zone</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {
            <span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>,
            <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>,
            <span class="pl-s">"width"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">zone_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.9</span>,  <span class="pl-c"># Leave 10% margin</span>
            <span class="pl-s">"height"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">zone_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.9</span>,
            <span class="pl-s">"group"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">group</span>
        }
        <span class="pl-s1">zones</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">zone</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">zones</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Within-Zone Node Positioning</h3><a id="user-content-3-within-zone-node-positioning" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Within-Zone Node Positioning" href="#3-within-zone-node-positioning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Position nodes within each zone:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option A: Organic Flow</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_organic(zone, nodes):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Organic, flowing arrangement within zone&quot;&quot;&quot;
    positions = []
    
    # Start at zone top-left with margin
    current_x = zone.x + 50
    current_y = zone.y + 50
    row_height = 0
    
    for node in nodes:
        # Check if node fits in current row
        if current_x + node.width &gt; zone.x + zone.width - 50:
            # Move to next row
            current_x = zone.x + 50
            current_y += row_height + VERTICAL_SPACING
            row_height = 0
        
        positions.append({
            &quot;x&quot;: current_x,
            &quot;y&quot;: current_y
        })
        
        current_x += node.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING
        row_height = max(row_height, node.height)
    
    return positions"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_organic</span>(<span class="pl-s1">zone</span>, <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Organic, flowing arrangement within zone"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">positions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Start at zone top-left with margin</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">row_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Check if node fits in current row</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span>:
            <span class="pl-c"># Move to next row</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">row_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">row_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">positions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({
            <span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span>,
            <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">current_y</span>
        })
        
        <span class="pl-s1">current_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">row_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">max</span>(<span class="pl-s1">row_height</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">positions</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option B: Structured Grid</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def position_grid(zone, nodes):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Grid arrangement within zone&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n = len(nodes)
    cols = ceil(sqrt(n))
    rows = ceil(n / cols)
    
    cell_width = (zone.width - 100) / cols  # 50px margin each side
    cell_height = (zone.height - 100) / rows
    
    positions = []
    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):
        col = i % cols
        row = i // cols
        
        # Center node in cell
        x = zone.x + 50 + col * cell_width + (cell_width - node.width) / 2
        y = zone.y + 50 + row * cell_height + (cell_height - node.height) / 2
        
        positions.append({&quot;x&quot;: x, &quot;y&quot;: y})
    
    return positions"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">position_grid</span>(<span class="pl-s1">zone</span>, <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Grid arrangement within zone"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">cols</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ceil</span>(<span class="pl-en">sqrt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n</span>))
    <span class="pl-s1">rows</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">ceil</span>(<span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-s1">cell_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>  <span class="pl-c"># 50px margin each side</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cell_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">rows</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">positions</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">//</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Center node in cell</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> (<span class="pl-s1">cell_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">zone</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> (<span class="pl-s1">cell_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">positions</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>({<span class="pl-s">"x"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s">"y"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">y</span>})
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">positions</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Cross-Zone Connections</h3><a id="user-content-4-cross-zone-connections" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Cross-Zone Connections" href="#4-cross-zone-connections"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Calculate optimal edge paths between zones:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def calculate_edge_path(from_node, to_node):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Determine edge connection points&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # Calculate centers
    from_center = (from_node.x + from_node.width/2, 
                   from_node.y + from_node.height/2)
    to_center = (to_node.x + to_node.width/2,
                 to_node.y + to_node.height/2)
    
    # Determine best sides to connect
    dx = to_center[0] - from_center[0]
    dy = to_center[1] - from_center[1]
    
    # Choose sides based on direction
    if abs(dx) &gt; abs(dy):
        # Horizontal connection
        from_side = &quot;right&quot; if dx &gt; 0 else &quot;left&quot;
        to_side = &quot;left&quot; if dx &gt; 0 else &quot;right&quot;
    else:
        # Vertical connection
        from_side = &quot;bottom&quot; if dy &gt; 0 else &quot;top&quot;
        to_side = &quot;top&quot; if dy &gt; 0 else &quot;bottom&quot;
    
    return {
        &quot;fromSide&quot;: from_side,
        &quot;toSide&quot;: to_side
    }"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">calculate_edge_path</span>(<span class="pl-s1">from_node</span>, <span class="pl-s1">to_node</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Determine edge connection points"""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Calculate centers</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">from_center</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">from_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">from_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>, 
                   <span class="pl-s1">from_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">from_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">to_center</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">to_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">to_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>,
                 <span class="pl-s1">to_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">to_node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span><span class="pl-c1">/</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Determine best sides to connect</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">to_center</span>[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>] <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">from_center</span>[<span class="pl-c1">0</span>]
    <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">to_center</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>] <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">from_center</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>]
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Choose sides based on direction</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">abs</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dx</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-en">abs</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dy</span>):
        <span class="pl-c"># Horizontal connection</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">from_side</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"right"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"left"</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">to_side</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"left"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"right"</span>
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Vertical connection</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">from_side</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"bottom"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"top"</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">to_side</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">"top"</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-s">"bottom"</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> {
        <span class="pl-s">"fromSide"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">from_side</span>,
        <span class="pl-s">"toSide"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">to_side</span>
    }</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Techniques</h2><a id="user-content-advanced-techniques" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Techniques" href="#advanced-techniques"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Force-Directed Layout</h3><a id="user-content-force-directed-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Force-Directed Layout" href="#force-directed-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For complex networks with many cross-connections:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def force_directed_layout(nodes, edges, iterations=100):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Spring-based layout algorithm&quot;&quot;&quot;
    # Constants
    SPRING_LENGTH = 200
    SPRING_CONSTANT = 0.1
    REPULSION_CONSTANT = 5000
    
    for iteration in range(iterations):
        # Calculate repulsive forces (all pairs)
        for node1 in nodes:
            force_x, force_y = 0, 0
            
            for node2 in nodes:
                if node1 == node2:
                    continue
                
                dx = node1.x - node2.x
                dy = node1.y - node2.y
                distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)
                
                if distance &gt; 0:
                    # Repulsive force
                    force = REPULSION_CONSTANT / (distance * distance)
                    force_x += (dx / distance) * force
                    force_y += (dy / distance) * force
            
            node1.force_x = force_x
            node1.force_y = force_y
        
        # Calculate attractive forces (connected nodes)
        for edge in edges:
            node1 = get_node(edge.fromNode)
            node2 = get_node(edge.toNode)
            
            dx = node2.x - node1.x
            dy = node2.y - node1.y
            distance = sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy)
            
            # Spring force
            force = SPRING_CONSTANT * (distance - SPRING_LENGTH)
            
            node1.force_x += (dx / distance) * force
            node1.force_y += (dy / distance) * force
            node2.force_x -= (dx / distance) * force
            node2.force_y -= (dy / distance) * force
        
        # Apply forces
        for node in nodes:
            node.x += node.force_x
            node.y += node.force_y"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">force_directed_layout</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">edges</span>, <span class="pl-s1">iterations</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">100</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Spring-based layout algorithm"""</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># Constants</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">SPRING_LENGTH</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">200</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">SPRING_CONSTANT</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.1</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">REPULSION_CONSTANT</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">5000</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">iteration</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">iterations</span>):
        <span class="pl-c"># Calculate repulsive forces (all pairs)</span>
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">force_x</span>, <span class="pl-s1">force_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
            
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>:
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>:
                    <span class="pl-k">continue</span>
                
                <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sqrt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dx</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dy</span>)
                
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>:
                    <span class="pl-c"># Repulsive force</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">force</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">REPULSION_CONSTANT</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> (<span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>)
                    <span class="pl-s1">force_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">force_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
            
            <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">force_x</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">force_y</span>
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Calculate attractive forces (connected nodes)</span>
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">edge</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">edges</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">node1</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_node</span>(<span class="pl-s1">edge</span>.<span class="pl-c1">fromNode</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">node2</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_node</span>(<span class="pl-s1">edge</span>.<span class="pl-c1">toNode</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">sqrt</span>(<span class="pl-s1">dx</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">dy</span><span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">dy</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-c"># Spring force</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">force</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">SPRING_CONSTANT</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-s1">distance</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">SPRING_LENGTH</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node1</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">-=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dx</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node2</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">-=</span> (<span class="pl-s1">dy</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">distance</span>) <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">force</span>
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Apply forces</span>
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_x</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">force_y</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Hierarchical Clustering</h3><a id="user-content-hierarchical-clustering" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Hierarchical Clustering" href="#hierarchical-clustering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Group related nodes automatically:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def hierarchical_cluster(nodes, similarity_threshold=0.7):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Cluster nodes by content similarity&quot;&quot;&quot;
    clusters = []
    
    # Calculate similarity matrix
    similarity = calculate_similarity_matrix(nodes)
    
    # Agglomerative clustering
    current_clusters = [[node] for node in nodes]
    
    while len(current_clusters) &gt; 1:
        # Find most similar clusters
        max_sim = 0
        merge_i, merge_j = 0, 1
        
        for i in range(len(current_clusters)):
            for j in range(i + 1, len(current_clusters)):
                sim = cluster_similarity(current_clusters[i], 
                                       current_clusters[j], 
                                       similarity)
                if sim &gt; max_sim:
                    max_sim = sim
                    merge_i, merge_j = i, j
        
        if max_sim &lt; similarity_threshold:
            break
        
        # Merge clusters
        current_clusters[merge_i].extend(current_clusters[merge_j])
        current_clusters.pop(merge_j)
    
    return current_clusters"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">hierarchical_cluster</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">similarity_threshold</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">0.7</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Cluster nodes by content similarity"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">clusters</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Calculate similarity matrix</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">similarity</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">calculate_similarity_matrix</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Agglomerative clustering</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> [[<span class="pl-s1">node</span>] <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>]
    
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Find most similar clusters</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">max_sim</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">merge_i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">merge_j</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
        
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>)):
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">j</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>, <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>)):
                <span class="pl-s1">sim</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">cluster_similarity</span>(<span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span>], 
                                       <span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>[<span class="pl-s1">j</span>], 
                                       <span class="pl-s1">similarity</span>)
                <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">sim</span> <span class="pl-c1">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">max_sim</span>:
                    <span class="pl-s1">max_sim</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">sim</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">merge_i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">merge_j</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">j</span>
        
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">max_sim</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">similarity_threshold</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">break</span>
        
        <span class="pl-c"># Merge clusters</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>[<span class="pl-s1">merge_i</span>].<span class="pl-c1">extend</span>(<span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>[<span class="pl-s1">merge_j</span>])
        <span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span>.<span class="pl-c1">pop</span>(<span class="pl-s1">merge_j</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">current_clusters</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Layout Optimization</h2><a id="user-content-layout-optimization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Layout Optimization" href="#layout-optimization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Minimize Edge Crossings</h3><a id="user-content-minimize-edge-crossings" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Minimize Edge Crossings" href="#minimize-edge-crossings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def minimize_crossings(nodes, edges):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Reduce edge crossing through node repositioning&quot;&quot;&quot;
    crossings = count_crossings(edges)
    
    # Try swapping adjacent nodes
    improved = True
    while improved:
        improved = False
        
        for i in range(len(nodes) - 1):
            # Swap nodes i and i+1
            swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])
            new_crossings = count_crossings(edges)
            
            if new_crossings &lt; crossings:
                crossings = new_crossings
                improved = True
            else:
                # Swap back
                swap_positions(nodes[i], nodes[i+1])"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">minimize_crossings</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">edges</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Reduce edge crossing through node repositioning"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">crossings</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">count_crossings</span>(<span class="pl-s1">edges</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Try swapping adjacent nodes</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">improved</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>
    <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-s1">improved</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">improved</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>
        
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>):
            <span class="pl-c"># Swap nodes i and i+1</span>
            <span class="pl-en">swap_positions</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span>], <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>])
            <span class="pl-s1">new_crossings</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">count_crossings</span>(<span class="pl-s1">edges</span>)
            
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">new_crossings</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s1">crossings</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">crossings</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">new_crossings</span>
                <span class="pl-s1">improved</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>
            <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
                <span class="pl-c"># Swap back</span>
                <span class="pl-en">swap_positions</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span>], <span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>])</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Visual Balance</h3><a id="user-content-visual-balance" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Visual Balance" href="#visual-balance"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def calculate_visual_weight(canvas):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Calculate center of mass for visual balance&quot;&quot;&quot;
    total_weight = 0
    weighted_x = 0
    weighted_y = 0
    
    for node in canvas.nodes:
        # Weight is proportional to area
        weight = node.width * node.height
        total_weight += weight
        
        weighted_x += node.center_x * weight
        weighted_y += node.center_y * weight
    
    center_x = weighted_x / total_weight
    center_y = weighted_y / total_weight
    
    # Shift entire canvas to center at (0, 0)
    offset_x = -center_x
    offset_y = -center_y
    
    for node in canvas.nodes:
        node.x += offset_x
        node.y += offset_y"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">calculate_visual_weight</span>(<span class="pl-s1">canvas</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Calculate center of mass for visual balance"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">total_weight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">weighted_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">weighted_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas</span>.<span class="pl-c1">nodes</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># Weight is proportional to area</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">weight</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">total_weight</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">weight</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">weighted_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">weight</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">weighted_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">center_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">weight</span>
    
    <span class="pl-s1">center_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">weighted_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">total_weight</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">center_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">weighted_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">total_weight</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"># Shift entire canvas to center at (0, 0)</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">offset_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-s1">center_x</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">offset_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-s1">center_y</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">canvas</span>.<span class="pl-c1">nodes</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">offset_x</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">offset_y</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Performance Optimization</h2><a id="user-content-performance-optimization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Performance Optimization" href="#performance-optimization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Spatial Indexing</h3><a id="user-content-spatial-indexing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Spatial Indexing" href="#spatial-indexing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For large canvases, use spatial indexing to speed up collision detection:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class SpatialGrid:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Grid-based spatial index for fast collision detection&quot;&quot;&quot;
    
    def __init__(self, cell_size=500):
        self.cell_size = cell_size
        self.grid = {}
    
    def add_node(self, node):
        &quot;&quot;&quot;Add node to grid&quot;&quot;&quot;
        cells = self.get_cells(node)
        for cell in cells:
            if cell not in self.grid:
                self.grid[cell] = []
            self.grid[cell].append(node)
    
    def get_cells(self, node):
        &quot;&quot;&quot;Get grid cells node occupies&quot;&quot;&quot;
        min_x = int(node.x / self.cell_size)
        max_x = int((node.x + node.width) / self.cell_size)
        min_y = int(node.y / self.cell_size)
        max_y = int((node.y + node.height) / self.cell_size)
        
        cells = []
        for x in range(min_x, max_x + 1):
            for y in range(min_y, max_y + 1):
                cells.append((x, y))
        return cells
    
    def get_nearby_nodes(self, node):
        &quot;&quot;&quot;Get nodes in nearby cells&quot;&quot;&quot;
        cells = self.get_cells(node)
        nearby = set()
        
        for cell in cells:
            if cell in self.grid:
                nearby.update(self.grid[cell])
        
        return nearby"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">SpatialGrid</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Grid-based spatial index for fast collision detection"""</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__init__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">cell_size</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">500</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cell_size</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell_size</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {}
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">add_node</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span>):
        <span class="pl-s">"""Add node to grid"""</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">cells</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_cells</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">cells</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell</span> <span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span></span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span>[<span class="pl-s1">cell</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
            <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span>[<span class="pl-s1">cell</span>].<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>)
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_cells</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span>):
        <span class="pl-s">"""Get grid cells node occupies"""</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">min_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cell_size</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">max_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>((<span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cell_size</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">min_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cell_size</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">max_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>((<span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span>) <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cell_size</span>)
        
        <span class="pl-s1">cells</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">min_x</span>, <span class="pl-s1">max_x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>):
            <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-s1">min_y</span>, <span class="pl-s1">max_y</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>):
                <span class="pl-s1">cells</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>((<span class="pl-s1">x</span>, <span class="pl-s1">y</span>))
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">cells</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get_nearby_nodes</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span>):
        <span class="pl-s">"""Get nodes in nearby cells"""</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">cells</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">get_cells</span>(<span class="pl-s1">node</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">nearby</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">set</span>()
        
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">cells</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">nearby</span>.<span class="pl-c1">update</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">grid</span>[<span class="pl-s1">cell</span>])
        
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s1">nearby</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Common Layout Patterns</h2><a id="user-content-common-layout-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Common Layout Patterns" href="#common-layout-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Timeline Layout</h3><a id="user-content-timeline-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Timeline Layout" href="#timeline-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For chronological content:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def layout_timeline(events, direction=&quot;horizontal&quot;):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Create timeline layout&quot;&quot;&quot;
    if direction == &quot;horizontal&quot;:
        for i, event in enumerate(events):
            event.x = i * (event.width + HORIZONTAL_SPACING)
            event.y = 0
    else:  # vertical
        for i, event in enumerate(events):
            event.x = 0
            event.y = i * (event.height + VERTICAL_SPACING)"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">layout_timeline</span>(<span class="pl-s1">events</span>, <span class="pl-s1">direction</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"horizontal"</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Create timeline layout"""</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">direction</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"horizontal"</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">event</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">events</span>):
            <span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">HORIZONTAL_SPACING</span>)
            <span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    <span class="pl-k">else</span>:  <span class="pl-c"># vertical</span>
        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">event</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">events</span>):
            <span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> (<span class="pl-s1">event</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">VERTICAL_SPACING</span>)</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Circular Layout</h3><a id="user-content-circular-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Circular Layout" href="#circular-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For cyclical processes:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def layout_circular(nodes, radius=500):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Arrange nodes in a circle&quot;&quot;&quot;
    n = len(nodes)
    angle_step = 2 * pi / n
    
    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):
        angle = i * angle_step
        node.x = radius * cos(angle) - node.width / 2
        node.y = radius * sin(angle) - node.height / 2"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">layout_circular</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">radius</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">500</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Arrange nodes in a circle"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">n</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">angle_step</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">pi</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-s1">n</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">angle</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">angle_step</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-en">cos</span>(<span class="pl-s1">angle</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">width</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">radius</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-en">sin</span>(<span class="pl-s1">angle</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">height</span> <span class="pl-c1">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Matrix Layout</h3><a id="user-content-matrix-layout" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Matrix Layout" href="#matrix-layout"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For comparing multiple dimensions:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def layout_matrix(nodes, rows, cols):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Arrange nodes in a matrix&quot;&quot;&quot;
    cell_width = 400
    cell_height = 250
    
    for i, node in enumerate(nodes):
        row = i // cols
        col = i % cols
        
        node.x = col * cell_width
        node.y = row * cell_height"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">layout_matrix</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>, <span class="pl-s1">rows</span>, <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""Arrange nodes in a matrix"""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cell_width</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">400</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cell_height</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">250</span>
    
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span>, <span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">enumerate</span>(<span class="pl-s1">nodes</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">//</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">%</span> <span class="pl-s1">cols</span>
        
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell_width</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">node</span>.<span class="pl-c1">y</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">row</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">cell_height</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quality Checks</h2><a id="user-content-quality-checks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quality Checks" href="#quality-checks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before finalizing layout, verify:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>No Overlaps</strong>: All nodes have minimum spacing</li>
<li><strong>Balanced</strong>: Visual center near (0, 0)</li>
<li><strong>Accessible</strong>: All nodes reachable via edges</li>

</ol>
